\n246: // synchronize is the main control loop that enforces eviction thresholds.\n247: // Returns the pod that was killed, or nil if no pod was killed.\n248: func (m *managerImpl) synchronize(ctx manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs\")\n265: \t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"eviction manager: failed to get HasDedicatedImageFs: %w\", imageFsErr)\n266: \t\t}\n267: \t\tm.dedicatedImageFs = filesystem\n271: \t\t\t// there is an error finding the split filesystem label and we want to ignore these errors\n272: \t\t\tlogger.Error(splitErr, \"eviction manager: failed to check if we have separate container filesystem. Ignoring.\")\n273: \t\t}\n274: \n275: \t\t// If we are a split filesystem but the feature is turned off\n276: \t\t// we should return an error.\n277: \t\t// This is a bad state.\n278: \t\tif !utilfeature.DefaultFeatureGate.Enabled(features.KubeletSeparateDiskGC) && splitContainerImageFs {\n279: \t\t\tsplitDiskError := fmt.Errorf(\"KubeletSeparateDiskGC is turned off but we still have a split filesystem\")\n280: \t\t\treturn nil, splitDiskError\n281: \t\t}\n282: \t\tthresholds, err := UpdateContainerFsThresholds(m.config.Thresholds, hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n283: \t\tm.config.Thresholds = thresholds\n284: \t\tif err != nil {\n285: \t\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"eviction manager: found conflicting containerfs eviction. Ignoring.\")\n286: \t\t}\n287: \t\tm.splitContainerImageFs = &splitContainerImageFs\n288: \t\tm.signalToRankFunc = buildSignalToRankFunc(hasImageFs, splitContainerImageFs)\n289: \"DedicatedImageFs\", m.dedicatedImageFs, \"SplitImageFs\", m.splitContainerImageFs)\n293: \tactivePods := podFunc()\n294: \tupdateStats := true\n295: \tsummary, err := m.summaryProvider.Get(ctx, updateStats)\n296: \tif err != nil {\n297: \t\tlogger.Error(err, \"Eviction manager: failed to get summary stats\")\n298: \t\treturn nil, nil\n299: \t}\n300: \n301: \tif \t\t}\n308: \t}\n309: \n310: \t// make observations and get a function to derive pod usage stats relative to those observations.\n311: \tobservations, statsFunc := makeSignalObservations(logger, summary)\n312: \tdebugLogObservations(logger, \"observations\", observations)\n313: \n314: \t// determine the set of thresholds met independent of grace period\n315: \tthresholds = thresholdsMet(logger, thresholds, observations, false)\n316: \tdebugLogThresholdsWithObservation(logger, \"thresholds - ignoring grace period\", thresholds, observations)\n317: \n318: \t// determine the set of thresholds previously met that have not yet satisfied the associated min-reclaim\n319: \tif len(m.thresholdsMet) > 0 {\n320: \t\tthresholdsNotYetResolved := thresholdsMet(logger,
